# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                       | HTTP Methods | Function Name             | Template Rendered           | Context Variables                                |
|-------------------------------|--------------|---------------------------|----------------------------|-------------------------------------------------|
| `/`                           | GET          | root                      | Redirects to `/dashboard`  | None                                            |
| `/dashboard`                  | GET          | dashboard_page            | dashboard.html             | devices_summary: dict (total:int, active:int, offline:int), rooms_summary: list of dict(room_name:str, device_count:int) |
| `/devices`                   | GET          | device_list_page          | devices.html               | devices: list of dict(device_id:int, name:str, type:str, room:str, status:str) |
| `/device/add`                | GET          | add_device_page           | add_device.html            | device_types: list of str, rooms: list of str                       |
| `/device/add`                | POST         | submit_add_device         | Redirects to `/devices`    | Form data: device_name (str), device_type (str), device_room (str)  |
| `/device/<int:device_id>`   | GET          | device_control_page       | device_control.html        | device: dict with device detail fields          |
| `/device/<int:device_id>/control` | POST   | post_device_control       | Redirects to `/devices` or `/device/<device_id>` | Form data for device control settings            |
| `/automation`                | GET          | automation_rules_page     | automation.html            | rules: list of dict with rule details, devices: list of dict for dropdown |
| `/automation`                | POST         | add_automation_rule       | Redirects to `/automation` | Form data for new automation rule                |
| `/energy`                   | GET          | energy_report_page        | energy_report.html         | energy_summary: dict(total_kwh: float, cost_estimate: float), energy_data: list of dict(date:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, consumption_kwh: float) |
| `/energy/filter`            | POST         | apply_energy_filter       | Redirects to `/energy`     | Form data: date filter (str)                     |
| `/activity`                 | GET          | activity_logs_page        | activity_logs.html         | activity_logs: list of dict(timestamp:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, action:str, details:str) |
| `/activity/search`          | POST         | search_activity_logs      | Redirects to `/activity`   | Form data: search query (str)                    |


**Details:**
- Root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- For device control routes, device_id is an integer parameter.
- POST routes handle form submissions.

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### 1. Dashboard Page
- Filepath: `templates/dashboard.html`
- Page Title: Smart Home Dashboard
- Element IDs:
  - `dashboard-page`: Div container for dashboard page
  - `device-summary`: Div showing total, active, and offline devices counts
  - `device-list-button`: Button to go to Device List page
  - `add-device-button`: Button to go to Add Device page
  - `automation-button`: Button to go to Automation Rules page
  - `energy-button`: Button to go to Energy Report page
  - `activity-button`: Button to go to Activity Logs page
  - `room-list`: Div showing list of rooms with device counts
- Navigation (all using `url_for`):
  - `device-list-button`: url_for('device_list_page')
  - `add-device-button`: url_for('add_device_page')
  - `automation-button`: url_for('automation_rules_page')
  - `energy-button`: url_for('energy_report_page')
  - `activity-button`: url_for('activity_logs_page')

### 2. Device List Page
- Filepath: `templates/devices.html`
- Page Title: My Devices
- Element IDs:
  - `device-list-page`: Div container
  - `device-table`: Table displaying devices
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}`: Button in each row with pattern `control-device-button-{device_id}` for device control. (Example: `control-device-button-1`)
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - Each `control-device-button-{device_id}`: url_for('device_control_page', device_id=device_id)
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 3. Add Device Page
- Filepath: `templates/add_device.html`
- Page Title: Add New Device
- Element IDs:
  - `add-device-page`: Div container
  - `device-name`: Input field for device name
  - `device-type`: Dropdown for device type selection
  - `device-room`: Dropdown for room selection
  - `submit-device-button`: Button to submit form
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 4. Device Control Page
- Filepath: `templates/device_control.html`
- Page Title: Device Control
- Element IDs:
  - `device-control-page`: Div container
  - `device-name-display`: H2 element for device name
  - `device-status-display`: Div displaying device status
  - `power-toggle`: Button to toggle power on/off
  - `save-settings-button`: Button to save settings
  - `back-to-devices`: Button to return to device list
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-devices`: url_for('device_list_page')

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- Filepath: `templates/automation.html`
- Page Title: Automation Rules
- Element IDs:
  - `automation-page`: Div container
  - `rules-table`: Table showing automation rules
  - `rule-name`: Input field for rule name
  - `trigger-type`: Dropdown for trigger type
  - `trigger-value`: Input field for trigger value
  - `action-device`: Dropdown for selecting device
  - `action-type`: Dropdown for action type
  - `add-rule-button`: Button to add new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 6. Energy Report Page
- Filepath: `templates/energy_report.html`
- Page Title: Energy Report
- Element IDs:
  - `energy-page`: Div container
  - `energy-summary`: Div showing total energy consumption and cost
  - `energy-table`: Table with energy consumption per device
  - `date-filter`: Date input for filtering
  - `apply-filter-button`: Button to apply filter
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- Filepath: `templates/activity_logs.html`
- Page Title: Activity Logs
- Element IDs:
  - `activity-page`: Div container
  - `activity-table`: Table showing activity logs
  - `search-activity`: Input text for searching logs
  - `apply-search-button`: Button to apply search
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. users.txt
- Filepath: `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. email (str)
- Description: Stores user account information.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### 2. devices.txt
- Filepath: `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. device_id (int)
  3. device_name (str)
  4. device_type (str) - e.g. Light, Thermostat
  5. room (str)
  6. brand (str)
  7. model (str)
  8. status (str) - Online/Offline
  9. power (str) - on/off
  10. brightness (str) - percentage or empty
  11. temperature (str) - degrees or empty
  12. mode (str) - e.g. Auto, Manual or empty
  13. schedule_time (str) - e.g. 22:00 or empty
- Description: Stores all devices owned by each user with detailed properties.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

### 3. rooms.txt
- Filepath: `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. room_id (int)
  3. room_name (str)
- Description: Stores rooms associated with each user.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

### 4. automation_rules.txt
- Filepath: `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. rule_id (int)
  3. rule_name (str)
  4. trigger_type (str) - Time, Motion, Temperature
  5. trigger_value (str)
  6. action_device_id (int)
  7. action_type (str) - Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature
  8. action_value (str) - might be empty
  9. enabled (str) - "true" or "false"
- Description: Stores automation rules for users.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

### 5. energy_logs.txt
- Filepath: `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. device_id (int)
  3. date (str) - YYYY-MM-DD
  4. consumption_kwh (float)
- Description: Records energy consumption per device per date.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

### 6. activity_logs.txt
- Filepath: `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. timestamp (str) - YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS
  3. device_id (int)
  4. action (str)
  5. details (str)
- Description: Logs all device activities and system events.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
```

---

This completes the full design specification for the SmartHomeManager web application.

                    <td>{{ rule.rule_name }}</td>
                    <td>{{ rule.trigger_type }}</td>
                    <td>{{ rule.trigger_value }}</td>
                    <td>{{ rule.action_device_name }}</td>
                    <td>{{ rule.action_type }}</td>
                    <td>{{ 'Yes' if rule.enabled == 'true' else 'No' }}</td>
                </tr>
                {% endfor %}
            </tbody>
        </table>
        <h2>Add New Rule</h2>
        <form method="POST" action="{{ url_for('add_automation_rule') }}">
            <label for="rule-name">Rule Name:</label>
            <input type="text" id="rule-name" name="rule_name" required><br><br>

            <label for="trigger-type">Trigger Type:</label>
            <select id="trigger-type" name="trigger_type" required>
                <option value="Time">Time</option>
                <option value="Motion">Motion</option>
                <option value="Temperature">Temperature</option>
            </select><br><br>

            <label for="trigger-value">Trigger Value:</label>
            <input type="text" id="trigger-value" name="trigger_value" required><br><br>

            <label for="action-device">Action Device:</label>
            <select id="action-device" name="action_device" required>
                {% for device in devices %}
                <option value="{{ device.device_id }}">{{ device.name }}</option>
                {% endfor %}
            </select><br><br>

            <label for="action-type">Action Type:</label>
            <select id="action-type" name="action_type" required>
                <option value="Turn On">Turn On</option>
                <option value="Turn Off">Turn Off</option>
                <option value="Set Brightness">Set Brightness</option>
                <option value="Set Temperature">Set Temperature</option>
            </select><br><br>

            <button type="submit" id="add-rule-button">Add Rule</button>
        </form>
        <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard_page') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
    </div>
</body>
</html>

Filepath: `data/users.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. email (str) - Description: Stores user account information. - Examples: ``` john_doe|john@example.com jane_smith|jane@example.com ```  ### 2. devices.txt - Filepath: `data/devices.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. device_id (int)   3. device_name (str)   4. device_type (str) - e.g. Light, Thermostat   5. room (str)   6. brand (str)   7. model (str)   8. status (str) - Online/Offline   9. power (str) - on/off   10. brightness (str) - percentage or empty   11. temperature (str) - degrees or empty   12. mode (str) - e.g. Auto, Manual or empty   13. schedule_time (str) - e.g. 22:00 or empty - Description: Stores all devices owned by each user with detailed properties. - Examples: ``` john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto| john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00 jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual| ```  ### 3. rooms.txt - Filepath: `data/rooms.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. room_id (int)   3. room_name (str) - Description: Stores rooms associated with each user. - Examples: ``` john_doe|1|Living Room john_doe|2|Bedroom john_doe|3|Kitchen jane_smith|1|Living Room ```  ### 4. automation_rules.txt - Filepath: `data/automation_rules.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. rule_id (int)   3. rule_name (str)   4. trigger_type (str) - Time, Motion, Temperature   5. trigger_value (str)   6. action_device_id (int)   7. action_type (str) - Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature   8. action_value (str) - might be empty   9. enabled (str) - "true" or "false" - Description: Stores automation rules for users. - Examples: ``` john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true ```  ### 5. energy_logs.txt - Filepath: `data/energy_logs.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. device_id (int)   3. date (str) - YYYY-MM-DD   4. consumption_kwh (float) - Description: Records energy consumption per device per date. - Examples: ``` john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5 john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3 john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6 jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2 ```  ### 6. activity_logs.txt - Filepath: `data/activity_logs.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. timestamp (str) - YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS   3. device_id (int)   4. action (str)   5. details (str) - Description: Logs all device activities and system events. - Examples: ``` john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72 jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control ```  ---  This completes the full design specification for the SmartHomeManager web application.

# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                       | HTTP Methods | Function Name             | Template Rendered           | Context Variables                                |
|-------------------------------|--------------|---------------------------|----------------------------|-------------------------------------------------|
| `/`                           | GET          | root                      | Redirects to `/dashboard`  | None                                            |
| `/dashboard`                  | GET          | dashboard_page            | dashboard.html             | devices_summary: dict (total:int, active:int, offline:int), rooms_summary: list of dict(room_name:str, device_count:int) |
| `/devices`                   | GET          | device_list_page          | devices.html               | devices: list of dict(device_id:int, name:str, type:str, room:str, status:str) |
| `/device/add`                | GET          | add_device_page           | add_device.html            | device_types: list of str, rooms: list of str                       |
| `/device/add`                | POST         | submit_add_device         | Redirects to `/devices`    | Form data: device_name (str), device_type (str), device_room (str)  |
| `/device/<int:device_id>`   | GET          | device_control_page       | device_control.html        | device: dict with device detail fields          |
| `/device/<int:device_id>/control` | POST   | post_device_control       | Redirects to `/devices` or `/device/<device_id>` | Form data for device control settings            |
| `/automation`                | GET          | automation_rules_page     | automation.html            | rules: list of dict with rule details, devices: list of dict for dropdown |
| `/automation`                | POST         | add_automation_rule       | Redirects to `/automation` | Form data for new automation rule                |
| `/energy`                   | GET          | energy_report_page        | energy_report.html         | energy_summary: dict(total_kwh: float, cost_estimate: float), energy_data: list of dict(date:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, consumption_kwh: float) |
| `/energy/filter`            | POST         | apply_energy_filter       | Redirects to `/energy`     | Form data: date filter (str)                     |
| `/activity`                 | GET          | activity_logs_page        | activity_logs.html         | activity_logs: list of dict(timestamp:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, action:str, details:str) |
| `/activity/search`          | POST         | search_activity_logs      | Redirects to `/activity`   | Form data: search query (str)                    |


**Details:**
- Root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- For device control routes, device_id is an integer parameter.
- POST routes handle form submissions.

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### 1. Dashboard Page
- Filepath: `templates/dashboard.html`
- Page Title: Smart Home Dashboard
- Element IDs:
  - `dashboard-page`: Div container for dashboard page
  - `device-summary`: Div showing total, active, and offline devices counts
  - `device-list-button`: Button to go to Device List page

  - `device-list-button`: url_for('device_list_page')
  - `add-device-button`: url_for('add_device_page')
  - `automation-button`: url_for('automation_rules_page')
  - `energy-button`: url_for('energy_report_page')
  - `activity-button`: url_for('activity_logs_page')

### 2. Device List Page

  - `device-table`: Table displaying devices
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}`: Button in each row with pattern `control-device-button-{device_id}` for device control. (Example: `control-device-button-1`)
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - Each `control-device-button-{device_id}`: url_for('device_control_page', device_id=device_id)
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 3. Add Device Page

- Page Title: Add New Device
- Element IDs:
  - `add-device-page`: Div container
  - `device-name`: Input field for device name
  - `device-type`: Dropdown for device type selection
  - `device-room`: Dropdown for room selection
  - `submit-device-button`: Button to submit form
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 4. Device Control Page
- Filepath: `templates/device_control.html`
- Page Title: Device Control
- Element IDs:
  - `device-control-page`: Div container
  - `device-name-display`: H2 element for device name
  - `device-status-display`: Div displaying device status
  - `power-toggle`: Button to toggle power on/off
  - `save-settings-button`: Button to save settings
  - `back-to-devices`: Button to return to device list
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-devices`: url_for('device_list_page')

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- Filepath: `templates/automation.html`
- Page Title: Automation Rules
- Element IDs:
  - `automation-page`: Div container
  - `rules-table`: Table showing automation rules
  - `rule-name`: Input field for rule name
  - `trigger-type`: Dropdown for trigger type
  - `trigger-value`: Input field for trigger value
  - `action-device`: Dropdown for selecting device

- Filepath: `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. email (str)
- Description: Stores user account information.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### 2. devices.txt
- Filepath: `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. device_id (int)
  3. device_name (str)
  4. device_type (str) - e.g. Light, Thermostat
  5. room (str)
  6. brand (str)
  7. model (str)
  8. status (str) - Online/Offline
  9. power (str) - on/off
  10. brightness (str) - percentage or empty
  11. temperature (str) - degrees or empty
  12. mode (str) - e.g. Auto, Manual or empty
  13. schedule_time (str) - e.g. 22:00 or empty
- Description: Stores all devices owned by each user with detailed properties.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

### 3. rooms.txt
- Filepath: `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. room_id (int)
  3. room_name (str)
- Description: Stores rooms associated with each user.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

### 4. automation_rules.txt
- Filepath: `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. rule_id (int)
  3. rule_name (str)
  4. trigger_type (str) - Time, Motion, Temperature
  5. trigger_value (str)
  6. action_device_id (int)
  7. action_type (str) - Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature
  8. action_value (str) - might be empty
  9. enabled (str) - "true" or "false"
- Description: Stores automation rules for users.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

### 5. energy_logs.txt
- Filepath: `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. device_id (int)
  3. date (str) - YYYY-MM-DD
  4. consumption_kwh (float)
- Description: Records energy consumption per device per date.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

### 6. activity_logs.txt
- Filepath: `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. timestamp (str) - YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS
  3. device_id (int)
  4. action (str)
  5. details (str)
- Description: Logs all device activities and system events.

```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights

# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                       | HTTP Methods | Function Name             | Template Rendered           | Context Variables                                |
|-------------------------------|--------------|---------------------------|----------------------------|-------------------------------------------------|
| `/`                           | GET          | root                      | Redirects to `/dashboard`  | None                                            |
| `/dashboard`                  | GET          | dashboard_page            | dashboard.html             | devices_summary: dict (total:int, active:int, offline:int), rooms_summary: list of dict(room_name:str, device_count:int) |
| `/devices`                   | GET          | device_list_page          | devices.html               | devices: list of dict(device_id:int, name:str, type:str, room:str, status:str) |
| `/device/add`                | GET          | add_device_page           | add_device.html            | device_types: list of str, rooms: list of str                       |
| `/device/add`                | POST         | submit_add_device         | Redirects to `/devices`    | Form data: device_name (str), device_type (str), device_room (str)  |
| `/device/<int:device_id>`   | GET          | device_control_page       | device_control.html        | device: dict with device detail fields          |
| `/device/<int:device_id>/control` | POST   | post_device_control       | Redirects to `/devices` or `/device/<device_id>` | Form data for device control settings            |
| `/automation`                | GET          | automation_rules_page     | automation.html            | rules: list of dict with rule details, devices: list of dict for dropdown |
| `/automation`                | POST         | add_automation_rule       | Redirects to `/automation` | Form data for new automation rule                |
| `/energy`                   | GET          | energy_report_page        | energy_report.html         | energy_summary: dict(total_kwh: float, cost_estimate: float), energy_data: list of dict(date:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, consumption_kwh: float) |
| `/energy/filter`            | POST         | apply_energy_filter       | Redirects to `/energy`     | Form data: date filter (str)                     |
| `/activity`                 | GET          | activity_logs_page        | activity_logs.html         | activity_logs: list of dict(timestamp:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, action:str, details:str) |
| `/activity/search`          | POST         | search_activity_logs      | Redirects to `/activity`   | Form data: search query (str)                    |


**Details:**
- Root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- For device control routes, device_id is an integer parameter.
- POST routes handle form submissions.

---

2. [21:00:33] LLM_RESPONSE
   Response: ```python
from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect
import os

app = Flask(__name__)
app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'

DATA_DIR = 'data'

# Utility functions to load pipe-delimited files as lists of lists
def load_pipe_delimited_file(filename):
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return []
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        lines = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    return [line.split('|') for line in lines]

# Utility function to write data (list of lists) back to file as pipe-delimited
def write_pipe_delimited_file(filename, data):
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for line in data:
            f.write('|'.join(str(x) for x in line) + '\n')


# -----------------------
# DASHBOARD ROUTE
# GET /
# Shows summary info of users, rooms, devices, energy for today
@app.route('/')
@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard_page():
    # Load rooms summary (assuming from rooms.txt + energy_logs.txt)
    # rooms.txt: room_id|room_name (?)
    rooms_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('rooms.txt')
    rooms = []
    for row in rooms_raw:
        if len(row) >= 2:
            rooms.append({'room_id': row[0], 'room_name': row[1]})

    # Devices summary: devices.txt stores device data pipe-delimited
    # devices.txt fields per line (assuming):
    # username|device_id|room_name|device_type|model|brand|status|on/off|brightness? etc.
    devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
    devices = []
    for d in devices_raw:
        if len(d) >= 7:
            devices.append({
                'username': d[0],
                'device_id': int(d[1]),
                'room_name': d[2],
                'device_type': d[3],
                'model': d[4],
                'brand': d[5],
                'status': d[6],  # On/off/offline/online etc.
            })

    # Energy summary: load today's energy usage from energy_logs.txt: date|device_id|kwh
    # We'll aggregate energy by room or device - show total energy per device for current day
    energy_logs = load_pipe_delimited_file('energy_logs.txt')
    from datetime import datetime
    today = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
    energy_summary = {}
    for log in energy_logs:
        if len(log) >= 4:
            username, device_id, date, kwh = log[0], int(log[1]), log[2], float(log[3])
            if date == today:
                energy_summary[device_id] = energy_summary.get(device_id, 0) + kwh

    return render_template('dashboard.html',
                           rooms=rooms,
                           devices=devices,
                           energy_summary=energy_summary,
                           today=today)


# -----------------------
# DEVICE LIST PAGE
# GET /devices
# Display all devices in a list with control buttons
@app.route('/devices')
def device_list_page():
    devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
    devices = []
    for d in devices_raw:
        if len(d) >= 7:
            devices.append({
                'username': d[0],
                'device_id': int(d[1]),
                'room_name': d[2],
                'device_type': d[3],
                'model': d[4],
                'brand': d[5],
                'status': d[6],
                'online': d[7] if len(d) > 7 else 'offline',
            })
    return render_template('devices.html', devices=devices)


# -----------------------
# DEVICE CONTROL PAGE
# GET and POST /device/<int:device_id>/control
# GET shows control interface; POST handles control form submissions on device
@app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def device_control_page(device_id):
    devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
    device = None
    idx = None
    for i, d in enumerate(devices_raw):
        if len(d) >= 2 and int(d[1]) == device_id:
            device = {
                'username': d[0],
                'device_id': int(d[1]),
                'room_name': d[2],
                'device_type': d[3],
                'model': d[4],
                'brand': d[5],
                'status': d[6],
                'online': d[7] if len(d) > 7 else 'offline',
            }
            idx = i
            break
    if device is None:
        return "Device not found", 404

    if request.method == 'POST':
        # Process control form: e.g. status on/off, brightness, etc.
        status = request.form.get('status', device['status'])
        # Update device status in devices_raw
        devices_raw[idx][6] = status
        write_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt', devices_raw)
        return redirect('/devices')

    return render_template('device_control.html', device=device)


# -----------------------
# ADD DEVICE PAGE
# GET and POST /device/add
# Form to add a new device
@app.route('/device/add', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def add_device_page():
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.form.get('username', '').strip()
        room_name = request.form.get('room_name', '').strip()
        device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()
        model = request.form.get('model', '').strip()
        brand = request.form.get('brand', '').strip()
        status = request.form.get('status', 'offline').strip()

        # Assign device_id as max existing id + 1
        devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
        max_id = 0
        for d in devices_raw:
            try:
                did = int(d[1])
                if did > max_id:
                    max_id = did
            except:
                pass
        new_id = max_id + 1

        new_device_line = [username, str(new_id), room_name, device_type, model, brand, status, 'offline']
        devices_raw.append(new_device_line)
        write_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt', devices_raw)

        return redirect('/devices')

    rooms_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('rooms.txt')
    rooms = [row[1] for row in rooms_raw if len(row) > 1]
    return render_template('add_device.html', rooms=rooms)


# -----------------------
# ENERGY REPORT PAGE
# GET /energy
# Optional filtering params: device_name, date_from, date_to
@app.route('/energy', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def energy_report_page():
    # POST or GET can be used for filter form submit
    # Load energy_logs.txt: username|device_id|date|kwh
    energy_logs = load_pipe_delimited_file('energy_logs.txt')

    # Get filter params
    device_name = request.values.get('device_name', '').strip()
    date_from = request.values.get('date_from', '').strip()
    date_to = request.values.get('date_to', '').strip()

    devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
    device_id_name_map = {}
    for d in devices_raw:
        if len(d) >= 5:
            device_id_name_map[int(d[1])] = d[3]  # device_type or name

    filtered_logs = []
    from datetime import datetime
    def parse_date(d):
        try:
            return datetime.strptime(d, '%Y-%m-%d')
        except:
            return None

    df = parse_date(date_from)
    dt = parse_date(date_to)

    for log in energy_logs:
        if len(log) < 4:
            continue
        username, device_id_str, date_str, kwh_str = log
        device_id_int = int(device_id_str)
        device_type = device_id_name_map.get(device_id_int, '')

        if device_name and device_name.lower() not in device_type.lower():
            continue
        log_date = parse_date(date_str)
        if df and (log_date is None or log_date < df):
            continue
        if dt and (log_date is None or log_date > dt):
            continue
        filtered_logs.append({
            'username': username,
            'device_id': device_id_int,
            'device_type': device_type,
            'date': date_str,
            'kwh': float(kwh_str)
        })

    return render_template('energy_report.html',
                           energy_logs=filtered_logs,
                           device_name=device_name,
                           date_from=date_from,
                           date_to=date_to)


# -----------------------
# ACTIVITY LOGS PAGE
# GET /activity
# Shows activity logs (from activity_logs.txt)
@app.route('/activity')
def activity_logs_page():
    activity_logs_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('activity_logs.txt')
    # Format: username|device_id|date|time|action_type|action_value
    activities = []
    for a in activity_logs_raw:
        if len(a) >= 6:
            activities.append({
                'username': a[0],
                'device_id': int(a[1]),
                'date': a[2],
                'time': a[3],
                'action_type': a[4],
                'action_value': a[5],
            })
    return render_template('activity_logs.html', activities=activities)


# -----------------------
# AUTOMATION RULES PAGE
# GET /automation
# Shows all automation rules and form to add new
@app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def automation_rules_page():
    if request.method == 'POST':
        rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()
        triggered_device_id = request.form.get('trigger_device_id', '').strip()
        action_device_id = request.form.get('action_device_id', '').strip()
        action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()
        action_value = request.form.get('action_value', '').strip()
        schedule_time = request.form.get('schedule_time', '').strip()
        enabled = request.form.get('enabled', 'false').lower() == 'true'

        rules_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('automation_rules.txt')
        max_rule_id = 0
        for r in rules_raw:
            try:
                rid = int(r[0])
                if rid > max_rule_id:
                    max_rule_id = rid
            except:
                pass
        new_rule_id = max_rule_id + 1

        new_rule_line = [str(new_rule_id), rule_name, triggered_device_id, action_device_id,
                         action_type, action_value, schedule_time, '1' if enabled else '0']
        rules_raw.append(new_rule_line)
        write_pipe_delimited_file('automation_rules.txt', rules_raw)
        return redirect('/automation')

    rules_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('automation_rules.txt')
    rules = []
    for r in rules_raw:
        if len(r) >= 8:
            rules.append({
                'rule_id': int(r[0]),
                'rule_name': r[1],
                'trigger_device_id': r[2],
                'action_device_id': r[3],
                'action_type': r[4],
                'action_value': r[5],
                'schedule_time': r[6],
                'enabled': r[7] == '1'
            })
    return render_template('automation.html', rules=rules)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(port=5000, debug=True)
```

=== design_spec.md ===
# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                       | HTTP Methods | Function Name             | Template Rendered           | Context Variables                                |
|-------------------------------|--------------|---------------------------|----------------------------|-------------------------------------------------|
| `/`                           | GET          | root                      | Redirects to `/dashboard`  | None                                            |
| `/dashboard`                  | GET          | dashboard_page            | dashboard.html             | devices_summary: dict (total:int, active:int, offline:int), rooms_summary: list of dict(room_name:str, device_count:int) |
| `/devices`                   | GET          | device_list_page          | devices.html               | devices: list of dict(device_id:int, name:str, type:str, room:str, status:str) |
| `/device/add`                | GET          | add_device_page           | add_device.html            | device_types: list of str, rooms: list of str                       |
| `/device/add`                | POST         | submit_add_device         | Redirects to `/devices`    | Form data: device_name (str), device_type (str), device_room (str)  |
| `/device/<int:device_id>`   | GET          | device_control_page       | device_control.html        | device: dict with device detail fields          |
| `/device/<int:device_id>/control` | POST   | post_device_control       | Redirects to `/devices` or `/device/<device_id>` | Form data for device control settings            |
| `/automation`                | GET          | automation_rules_page     | automation.html            | rules: list of dict with rule details, devices: list of dict for dropdown |
| `/automation`                | POST         | add_automation_rule       | Redirects to `/automation` | Form data for new automation rule                |
| `/energy`                   | GET          | energy_report_page        | energy_report.html         | energy_summary: dict(total_kwh: float, cost_estimate: float), energy_data: list of dict(date:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, consumption_kwh: float) |
| `/energy/filter`            | POST         | apply_energy_filter       | Redirects to `/energy`     | Form data: date filter (str)                     |
| `/activity`                 | GET          | activity_logs_page        | activity_logs.html         | activity_logs: list of dict(timestamp:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, action:str, details:str) |
| `/activity/search`          | POST         | search_activity_logs      | Redirects to `/activity`   | Form data: search query (str)                    |


**Details:**
- Root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- For device control routes, device_id is an integer parameter.
- POST routes handle form submissions.

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. users.txt
- Filepath: `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. email (str)
- Description: Stores user account information.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### 2. devices.txt
- Filepath: `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. device_id (int)
  3. device_name (str)
  4. device_type (str) - e.g. Light, Thermostat
  5. room (str)
  6. brand (str)
  7. model (str)
  8. status (str) - Online/Offline
  9. power (str) - on/off
  10. brightness (str) - percentage or empty
  11. temperature (str) - degrees or empty
  12. mode (str) - e.g. Auto, Manual or empty
  13. schedule_time (str) - e.g. 22:00 or empty
- Description: Stores all devices owned by each user with detailed properties.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

### 3. rooms.txt
- Filepath: `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. room_id (int)
  3. room_name (str)
- Description: Stores rooms associated with each user.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

### 4. automation_rules.txt
- Filepath: `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. rule_id (int)
  3. rule_name (str)
  4. trigger_type (str) - Time, Motion, Temperature
  5. trigger_value (str)
  6. action_device_id (int)
  7. action_type (str) - Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature
  8. action_value (str) - might be empty
  9. enabled (str) - "true" or "false"
- Description: Stores automation rules for users.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

### 5. energy_logs.txt
- Filepath: `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. device_id (int)
  3. date (str) - YYYY-MM-DD
  4. consumption_kwh (float)
- Description: Records energy consumption per device per date.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

### 6. activity_logs.txt
- Filepath: `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. username (str)
  2. timestamp (str) - YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS
  3. device_id (int)
  4. action (str)
  5. details (str)
- Description: Logs all device activities and system events.
- Examples:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
```

---

This completes the full design specification for the SmartHomeManager web application.

   Response: ```python
from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'

DATA_DIR = 'data'


def load_pipe_delimited_file(filename):
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return []
    with open(path, encoding='utf-8') as f:
        lines = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    return [line.split('|') for line in lines]


def write_pipe_delimited_file(filename, data):
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for line in data:
            f.write('|'.join(str(x) for x in line) + '\n')


@app.route('/')
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))


@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard_page():
    # Load rooms for summary
    rooms_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('rooms.txt')
    rooms = [{'room_id': r[0], 'room_name': r[1]} for r in rooms_raw if len(r) >= 2]

    # Load devices summary
    devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
    devices = []
    for d in devices_raw:
        if len(d) >= 7:
            try:
                devices.append({
                    'username': d[0],
                    'device_id': int(d[1]),
                    'room_name': d[2],
                    'device_type': d[3],
                    'model': d[4],
                    'brand': d[5],
                    'status': d[6],
                    'online': d[7] if len(d) > 7 else 'offline',
                })
            except Exception:
                continue

    # Load energy logs - aggregate by device for today
    energy_logs_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('energy_logs.txt')
    today = datetime.today().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
    energy_summary = {}
    for record in energy_logs_raw:
        if len(record) < 4:
            continue
        try:
            _, device_id_s, date_str, kwh_s = record[:4]
            device_id = int(device_id_s)
            kwh = float(kwh_s)
            if date_str == today:
                energy_summary[device_id] = energy_summary.get(device_id, 0.0) + kwh
        except Exception:
            continue

    return render_template('dashboard.html', rooms=rooms, devices=devices,
                           energy_summary=energy_summary, today=today)


@app.route('/devices')
def device_list_page():
    devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
    devices = []
    for d in devices_raw:
        if len(d) >= 7:
            try:
                devices.append({
                    'username': d[0],
                    'device_id': int(d[1]),
                    'room_name': d[2],
                    'device_type': d[3],
                    'model': d[4],
                    'brand': d[5],
                    'status': d[6],
                    'online': d[7] if len(d) > 7 else 'offline'
                })
            except Exception:
                continue
    return render_template('devices.html', devices=devices)


@app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def device_control_page(device_id):
    devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
    device = None
    index = None
    for i, d in enumerate(devices_raw):
        try:
            if len(d) >= 2 and int(d[1]) == device_id:
                device = d
                index = i
                break
        except Exception:
            continue
    if device is None:
        return "Device not found", 404

    if request.method == 'POST':
        status = request.form.get('status')
        # Update status field in line index: 6th index (status)
        if status is not None:
            devices_raw[index][6] = status
            write_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt', devices_raw)
        return redirect(url_for('device_list_page'))

    device_data = {
        'username': device[0],
        'device_id': int(device[1]),
        'room_name': device[2],
        'device_type': device[3],
        'model': device[4],
        'brand': device[5],
        'status': device[6],
        'online': device[7] if len(device) > 7 else 'offline',
    }
    return render_template('device_control.html', device=device_data)


@app.route('/device/add', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def add_device_page():
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.form.get('username', '').strip()
        room_name = request.form.get('room_name', '').strip()
        device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()
        model = request.form.get('model', '').strip()
        brand = request.form.get('brand', '').strip()
        status = request.form.get('status', 'offline').strip()

        devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
        max_id = 0
        for d in devices_raw:
            try:
                id_ = int(d[1])
                if id_ > max_id:
                    max_id = id_
            except Exception:
                continue
        new_id = max_id + 1
        new_entry = [username, str(new_id), room_name, device_type, model, brand, status, 'offline']
        devices_raw.append(new_entry)
        write_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt', devices_raw)
        return redirect(url_for('device_list_page'))

    rooms_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('rooms.txt')
    rooms = [r[1] for r in rooms_raw if len(r) > 1]
    return render_template('add_device.html', rooms=rooms)


@app.route('/energy', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def energy_report_page():
    energy_logs_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('energy_logs.txt')
    devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')
    device_map = {}
    for d in devices_raw:
        if len(d) >= 5:
            try:
                device_id = int(d[1])
                device_map[device_id] = d[3]  # device_type used as name
            except Exception:
                continue

    device_name_filter = request.values.get('device_name', '').strip().lower()
    date_from = request.values.get('date_from', '').strip()
    date_to = request.values.get('date_to', '').strip()

    def parse_date_safe(d):
        try:
            return datetime.strptime(d, '%Y-%m-%d')
        except Exception:
            return None

    dt_from = parse_date_safe(date_from)
    dt_to = parse_date_safe(date_to)

    entries = []
    for record in energy_logs_raw:
        if len(record) < 4:
            continue
        try:
            username, device_id_s, date_s, kwh_s = record[:4]
            device_id = int(device_id_s)
            device_type = device_map.get(device_id, '')
            if device_name_filter and device_name_filter not in device_type.lower():
                continue
            date_obj = parse_date_safe(date_s)
            if dt_from and (date_obj is None or date_obj < dt_from):
                continue
            if dt_to and (date_obj is None or date_obj > dt_to):
                continue
            entries.append({
                'username': username,
                'device_id': device_id,
                'device_type': device_type,
                'date': date_s,
                'kwh': float(kwh_s)
            })
        except Exception:
            continue

    return render_template('energy_report.html',
                           energy_logs=entries,
                           device_name=device_name_filter,
                           date_from=date_from,
                           date_to=date_to)


@app.route('/activity')
def activity_logs_page():
    activity_logs_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('activity_logs.txt')
    activities = []
    for a in activity_logs_raw:
        if len(a) >= 6:
            try:
                activities.append({
                    'username': a[0],
                    'device_id': int(a[1]),
                    'date': a[2],
                    'time': a[3],
                    'action_type': a[4],
                    'action_value': a[5],
                })
            except Exception:
                continue
    return render_template('activity_logs.html', activities=activities)


@app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def automation_rules_page():
    if request.method == 'POST':
        rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()
        trigger_device_id = request.form.get('trigger_device_id', '').strip()
        action_device_id = request.form.get('action_device_id', '').strip()
        action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()
        action_value = request.form.get('action_value', '').strip()
        schedule_time = request.form.get('schedule_time', '').strip()
        enabled = request.form.get('enabled', 'false').lower() == 'true'

        rules_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('automation_rules.txt')
        max_rule_id = 0
        for r in rules_raw:
            try:
                rid = int(r[0])
                if rid > max_rule_id:
                    max_rule_id = rid
            except Exception:
                continue
        new_rule_id = max_rule_id + 1
        new_line = [str(new_rule_id), rule_name, trigger_device_id, action_device_id, action_type,
                    action_value, schedule_time, '1' if enabled else '0']
        rules_raw.append(new_line)
        write_pipe_delimited_file('automation_rules.txt', rules_raw)

        return redirect(url_for('automation_rules_page'))

    rules_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('automation_rules.txt')
    rules = []
    for r in rules_raw:
        if len(r) >= 8:
            try:
                rules.append({
                    'rule_id': int(r[0]),
                    'rule_name': r[1],
                    'trigger_device_id': r[2],
                    'action_device_id': r[3],
                    'action_type': r[4],
                    'action_value': r[5],
                    'schedule_time': r[6],
                    'enabled': r[7] == '1'
                })
            except Exception:
                continue
    return render_template('automation.html', rules=rules)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(port=5000, debug=True)

`/` redirects to `/dashboard`. - For device control routes, device_id is an integer parameter. - POST routes handle form submissions.  ---  ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification  ### 1. Dashboard Page - Filepath: `templates/dashboard.html` - Page Title: Smart Home Dashboard - Element IDs:   - `dashboard-page`: Div container for dashboard page   - `device-summary`: Div showing total, active, and offline devices counts   - `device-list-button`: Button to go to Device List page   - `add-device-button`: Button to go to Add Device page   - `automation-button`: Button to go to Automation Rules page   - `energy-button`: Button to go to Energy Report page   - `activity-button`: Button to go to Activity Logs page   - `room-list`: Div showing list of rooms with device counts - Navigation (all using `url_for`):   - `device-list-button`: url_for('device_list_page')   - `add-device-button`: url_for('add_device_page')   - `automation-button`: url_for('automation_rules_page')   - `energy-button`: url_for('energy_report_page')   - `activity-button`: url_for('activity_logs_page')  ### 2. Device List Page - Filepath: `templates/devices.html` - Page Title: My Devices - Element IDs:   - `device-list-page`: Div container   - `device-table`: Table displaying devices   - `control-device-button-{device_id}`: Button in each row with pattern `control-device-button-{device_id}` for device control. (Example: `control-device-button-1`)   - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard - Navigation:   - Each `control-device-button-{device_id}`: url_for('device_control_page', device_id=device_id)   - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')  ### 3. Add Device Page - Filepath: `templates/add_device.html` - Page Title: Add New Device - Element IDs:   - `add-device-page`: Div container   - `device-name`: Input field for device name   - `device-type`: Dropdown for device type selection   - `device-room`: Dropdown for room selection   - `submit-device-button`: Button to submit form   - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard - Navigation:   - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')  ### 4. Device Control Page - Filepath: `templates/device_control.html` - Page Title: Device Control - Element IDs:   - `device-control-page`: Div container   - `device-name-display`: H2 element for device name   - `device-status-display`: Div displaying device status   - `power-toggle`: Button to toggle power on/off   - `save-settings-button`: Button to save settings   - `back-to-devices`: Button to return to device list - Navigation:   - `back-to-devices`: url_for('device_list_page')  ### 5. Automation Rules Page - Filepath: `templates/automation.html` - Page Title: Automation Rules - Element IDs:   - `automation-page`: Div container   - `rules-table`: Table showing automation rules   - `rule-name`: Input field for rule name   - `trigger-type`: Dropdown for trigger type   - `trigger-value`: Input field for trigger value   - `action-device`: Dropdown for selecting device   - `action-type`: Dropdown for action type   - `add-rule-button`: Button to add new rule   - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard - Navigation:   - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')  ### 6. Energy Report Page - Filepath: `templates/energy_report.html` - Page Title: Energy Report - Element IDs:   - `energy-page`: Div container   - `energy-summary`: Div showing total energy consumption and cost   - `energy-table`: Table with energy consumption per device   - `date-filter`: Date input for filtering   - `apply-filter-button`: Button to apply filter   - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard - Navigation:   - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')  ### 7. Activity Logs Page - Filepath: `templates/activity_logs.html` - Page Title: Activity Logs - Element IDs:   - `activity-page`: Div container   - `activity-table`: Table showing activity logs   - `search-activity`: Input text for searching logs   - `apply-search-button`: Button to apply search   - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard - Navigation:   - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')  ---  ## Section 3: Data File Schemas  ### 1. users.txt - Filepath: `data/users.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. email (str) - Description: Stores user account information. - Examples: ``` john_doe|john@example.com jane_smith|jane@example.com ```  ### 2. devices.txt - Filepath: `data/devices.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. device_id (int)   3. device_name (str)   4. device_type (str) - e.g. Light, Thermostat   5. room (str)   6. brand (str)   7. model (str)   8. status (str) - Online/Offline   9. power (str) - on/off   10. brightness (str) - percentage or empty   11. temperature (str) - degrees or empty   12. mode (str) - e.g. Auto, Manual or empty   13. schedule_time (str) - e.g. 22:00 or empty - Description: Stores all devices owned by each user with detailed properties. - Examples: ``` john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto| john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00 jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual| ```  ### 3. rooms.txt - Filepath: `data/rooms.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. room_id (int)   3. room_name (str) - Description: Stores rooms associated with each user. - Examples: ``` john_doe|1|Living Room john_doe|2|Bedroom john_doe|3|Kitchen jane_smith|1|Living Room ```  ### 4. automation_rules.txt - Filepath: `data/automation_rules.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. rule_id (int)   3. rule_name (str)   4. trigger_type (str) - Time, Motion, Temperature   5. trigger_value (str)   6. action_device_id (int)   7. action_type (str) - Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature   8. action_value (str) - might be empty   9. enabled (str) - "true" or "false" - Description: Stores automation rules for users. - Examples: ``` john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true ```  ### 5. energy_logs.txt - Filepath: `data/energy_logs.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. device_id (int)   3. date (str) - YYYY-MM-DD   4. consumption_kwh (float) - Description: Records energy consumption per device per date. - Examples: ``` john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5 john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3 john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6 jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2 ```  ### 6. activity_logs.txt - Filepath: `data/activity_logs.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   1. username (str)   2. timestamp (str) - YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS   3. device_id (int)   4. action (str)   5. details (str) - Description: Logs all device activities and system events. - Examples: ``` john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72 jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control ```  ---  This completes the full design specification for the SmartHomeManager web application.

'data'   def load_pipe_delimited_file(filename):     path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)     if not os.path.exists(path):         return []     with open(path, encoding='utf-8') as f:         lines = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]     return [line.split('|') for line in lines]   def write_pipe_delimited_file(filename, data):     path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)     with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:         for line in data:             f.write('|'.join(str(x) for x in line) + '\n')   @app.route('/') def root():     return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))   @app.route('/dashboard') def dashboard_page():     # Load devices to calculate total, active, offline     devices_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('devices.txt')     total = 0     active = 0     offline = 0     for d in devices_raw:         if len(d) < 9:             continue         status = d[7].strip()         power = d[8].strip() if len(d) > 8 else ''         total += 1         if status.lower() == 'online' and power.lower() == 'on':             active += 1         elif status.lower() == 'offline':             offline += 1      devices_summary = {'total': total, 'active': active, 'offline': offline}      # Rooms summary: count devices per room     rooms_raw = load_pipe_delimited_file('rooms.txt')     rooms_summary = []     # Collect rooms for all users (aggregate by room name)     rooms_count = {}     for room_line in rooms_raw:         if len(room_line) < 3:             continue         username, room_id, room_name = room_line[0], room_line[1], room_line[2]         if room_name not in rooms_count:             rooms_count[room_name] = 0     for d in devices_raw:         if len(d) < 5:             continue         room = d[4].strip()         if room in rooms_count:             rooms_count[room] += 1     for room_name, count in rooms_count.items():         rooms_summary.append({'room_name': room_name, 'device_count': count})      return # SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                       | HTTP Methods | Function Name             | Template Rendered           | Context Variables                                |
|-------------------------------|--------------|---------------------------|----------------------------|-------------------------------------------------|
| `/`                           | GET          | root                      | Redirects to `/dashboard`  | None                                            |
| `/dashboard`                  | GET          | dashboard_page            | dashboard.html             | devices_summary: dict (total:int, active:int, offline:int), rooms_summary: list of dict(room_name:str, device_count:int) |
| `/devices`                   | GET          | device_list_page          | devices.html               | devices: list of dict(device_id:int, name:str, type:str, room:str, status:str) |
| `/device/add`                | GET          | add_device_page           | add_device.html            | device_types: list of str, rooms: list of str                       |
| `/device/add`                | POST         | submit_add_device         | Redirects to `/devices`    | Form data: device_name (str), device_type (str), device_room (str)  |
| `/device/<int:device_id>`   | GET          | device_control_page       | device_control.html        | device: dict with device detail fields          |
| `/device/<int:device_id>/control` | POST   | post_device_control       | Redirects to `/devices` or `/device/<device_id>` | Form data for device control settings            |
| `/automation`                | GET          | automation_rules_page     | automation.html            | rules: list of dict with rule details, devices: list of dict for dropdown |
| `/automation`                | POST         | add_automation_rule       | Redirects to `/automation` | Form data for new automation rule                |
| `/energy`                   | GET          | energy_report_page        | energy_report.html         | energy_summary: dict(total_kwh: float, cost_estimate: float), energy_data: list of dict(date:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, consumption_kwh: float) |
| `/energy/filter`            | POST         | apply_energy_filter       | Redirects to `/energy`     | Form data: date filter (str)                     |
| `/activity`                 | GET          | activity_logs_page        | activity_logs.html         | activity_logs: list of dict(timestamp:str, device_id:int, device_name:str, action:str, details:str) |
| `/activity/search`          | POST         | search_activity_logs      | Redirects to `/activity`   | Form data: search query (str)                    |


**Details:**
- Root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- For device control routes, device_id is an integer parameter.
- POST routes handle form submissions.

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### 1. Dashboard Page
- Filepath: `templates/dashboard.html`
- Page Title: Smart Home Dashboard
- Element IDs:
  - `dashboard-page`: Div container for dashboard page
  - `device-summary`: Div showing total, active, and offline devices counts
  - `device-list-button`: Button to go to Device List page
  - `add-device-button`: Button to go to Add Device page
  - `automation-button`: Button to go to Automation Rules page
  - `energy-button`: Button to go to Energy Report page
  - `activity-button`: Button to go to Activity Logs page
  - `room-list`: Div showing list of rooms with device counts
- Navigation (all using `url_for`):
  - `device-list-button`: url_for('device_list_page')
  - `add-device-button`: url_for('add_device_page')
  - `automation-button`: url_for('automation_rules_page')
  - `energy-button`: url_for('energy_report_page')
  - `activity-button`: url_for('activity_logs_page')

### 2. Device List Page
- Filepath: `templates/devices.html`
- Page Title: My Devices
- Element IDs:
  - `device-list-page`: Div container
  - `device-table`: Table displaying devices
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}`: Button in each row with pattern `control-device-button-{device_id}` for device control. (Example: `control-device-button-1`)
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - Each `control-device-button-{device_id}`: url_for('device_control_page', device_id=device_id)
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 3. Add Device Page
- Filepath: `templates/add_device.html`
- Page Title: Add New Device
- Element IDs:
  - `add-device-page`: Div container
  - `device-name`: Input field for device name
  - `device-type`: Dropdown for device type selection
  - `device-room`: Dropdown for room selection
  - `submit-device-button`: Button to submit form
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 4. Device Control Page
- Filepath: `templates/device_control.html`
- Page Title: Device Control
- Element IDs:
  - `device-control-page`: Div container
  - `device-name-display`: H2 element for device name
  - `device-status-display`: Div displaying device status
  - `power-toggle`: Button to toggle power on/off
  - `save-settings-button`: Button to save settings
  - `back-to-devices`: Button to return to device list
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-devices`: url_for('device_list_page')

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- Filepath: `templates/automation.html`
- Page Title: Automation Rules
- Element IDs:
  - `automation-page`: Div container
  - `rules-table`: Table showing automation rules
  - `rule-name`: Input field for rule name
  - `trigger-type`: Dropdown for trigger type
  - `trigger-value`: Input field for trigger value
  - `action-device`: Dropdown for selecting device
  - `action-type`: Dropdown for action type
  - `add-rule-button`: Button to add new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 6. Energy Report Page
- Filepath: `templates/energy_report.html`
- Page Title: Energy Report
- Element IDs:
  - `energy-page`: Div container
  - `energy-summary`: Div showing total energy consumption and cost
  - `energy-table`: Table with energy consumption per device
  - `date-filter`: Date input for filtering
  - `apply-filter-button`: Button to apply filter
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- Filepath: `templates/activity_logs.html`
- Page Title: Activity Logs
- Element IDs:
  - `activity-page`: Div container
  - `activity-table`: Table showing activity logs
  - `search-activity`: Input text for searching logs
  - `apply-search-button`: Button to apply search
  - `back-to-dashboard`: Button to go to Dashboard
- Navigation:
  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard_page')
